# [Archived] Architectural Assessment & Implementation Plan

> **Date:** 2026-05-05
> **Session ID:** `d7f00fdb`

---

## 1. Implementation Plan

# Architectural Assessment & Implementation Plan

Based on the audit criteria provided and the principles in `AI_PROFILE.md`, here is a thorough assessment of the current system architecture and proposed fixes.

## User Review Required

Please review the assessments below. If you approve, I will proceed to implement the **Phase A (High-Impact)** changes in the next step.

## Assessment Findings

### 1. 效能與本地模型優化 (Performance & Local LLM)
- **模型路由最佳化 (Model Routing)**: 
  - *Current State*: `router_agent.py` routes tasks to skills, but the skills hardcode the model inside their `config.yaml`. There is no context-aware model switching.
  - *Assessment*: **Valid Issue**. We should update the Router to dynamically pass a `--model` flag (or context) so lightweight tasks use Qwen-7B and complex tasks use DeepSeek-R1.
- **語意快取 (Semantic Caching)**:
  - *Current State*: `llm_client.py` sends every prompt to Ollama, even if identical.
  - *Assessment*: **Valid Issue**. Implementing a lightweight SQLite/Redis cache inside `llm_client.py` will save significant GPU time.

### 2. 記憶與知識圖譜強化 (Memory & Graph)
- **混合檢索 (Hybrid Retrieval)**:
  - *Current State*: **Already Implemented** in V9.0 (`hybrid_retriever.py` combines ChromaDB and NetworkX).
- **動態記憶衰退 (Dynamic Memory Decay)**:
  - *Current State*: Not implemented.
  - *Assessment*: **Valid Future Feature**. We can implement a time-decay weight in `session_state.py` or the retriever.

### 3. 架構與防錯處理 (Robustness)
- **重試與容錯機制 (Exponential Backoff in Task Queue)**:
  - *Current State*: `llm_client.py` uses `tenacity` for backoff, but `task_queue.py` only has a basic `max_retries = 3` loop.
  - *Assessment*: **Valid Issue**. We should add an exponential backoff decorator to the async/subprocess dispatch in `task_queue.py`.
- **資料隔離設計 (Quarantine)**:
  - *Current State*: **Already Implemented**. `task_queue.py` has a `_quarantine_file` method that automatically moves failed PDFs/audio to `data/quarantine/<skill>` after 3 failures and notifies via Telegram.

### 4. 安全性 (Security)
- **ChromaDB SQLite 暴露風險**:
  - *Current State*: It is stored locally.
  - *Assessment*: Since it's a local-first system, this is acceptable for now. If an API layer is added later, JWT authentication will be required.

### 5. 局限性 (Limitations)
- **硬體依賴與排程器衝突 (Hardware Bottleneck)**:
  - *Current State*: `scheduler.py` might trigger processes concurrently with `inbox_daemon`.
  - *Assessment*: **Valid Issue**. We must ensure `scheduler.py` dispatches its heavy tasks directly into the single-threaded `LocalTaskQueue` rather than spawning its own subprocesses.
- **狀態管理鎖 (File IO Lock)**:
  - *Current State*: `JsonStateBackend` uses `fcntl.flock(EX)`. This is safe but blocking.
  - *Assessment*: **Already Solved Architecturally**. `state_backend.py` already includes a `RedisStateBackend`. Users experiencing File IO locks can simply change `config.yaml` to `type: "redis"` to enable atomic Redis MULTI/EXEC locks without code changes.

---

## Proposed Implementation Plan

### Phase A: High-Impact Optimizations (Recommended Now)
1. **Semantic Caching in `llm_client.py`**: Add a lightweight SQLite dictionary to cache identical `(model, prompt, temperature=0)` pairs.
2. **Context-Aware Routing in `router_agent.py`**: Modify the router to determine `complexity: low | high` and dispatch appropriate model overrides to the downstream skills.
3. **Task Queue Exponential Backoff**: Add `tenacity` retry backoff inside `task_queue.py` for subprocess execution.
4. **Scheduler Queue Safety**: Ensure `scheduler.py` uses `task_queue.enqueue()` for all Anki and heavy tasks instead of running them synchronously.

### Phase B: Advanced Features (Future Scope)
1. Dynamic Memory Decay (Time-weighted retrieval).
2. JWT Authentication Layer for API.

## Open Questions

1. Should I proceed with implementing **Phase A** immediately?
2. For Semantic Caching, do you prefer a zero-dependency **SQLite** cache, or since Redis is already supported in `state_backend`, should we use **Redis**?


---

## 2. Walkthrough / Summary

# Phase A: High-Impact Architecture Optimizations Walkthrough

> **Completed:** 2026-05-04

We have successfully completed all Phase A tasks to enhance the performance, routing intelligence, and robustness of the Open Claw ecosystem.

## Key Accomplishments

### 1. Semantic Caching (`llm_client.py`)
- Implemented a zero-dependency `SqliteSemanticCache`.
- Stored at `data/llm_cache.sqlite3` to natively persist across reboots.
- The `OllamaClient` now intercepts deterministic generation requests (`temperature=0`) and directly returns the cached output if a `model::prompt` hash matches.
- Dramatically reduces local GPU rendering time for redundant academic and routing queries.

### 2. Context-Aware Model Routing (`router_agent.py`)
- The `RouterAgent` now analyzes user intents against a complexity keyword matrix (`debate`, `research`, `feynman`, `analyze`, `deep`, `study`).
- **Low Complexity** (e.g. transcribing, basic summaries) defaults to `qwen2.5-coder:7b`.
- **High Complexity** (e.g. Feynman Simulator debates, deep academic research) automatically overrides the model to `deepseek-r1:14b`.
- The selected model is injected into the subprocess via the `OPENCLAW_ROUTER_MODEL` environment variable, ensuring the downstream Skill seamlessly picks up the instruction.

### 3. Task Queue Exponential Backoff (`task_queue.py`)
- Upgraded the `LocalTaskQueue._worker_loop` to support `env` parameter injection.
- Added a robust `time.sleep` exponential backoff (`5 * 2^retry_count` seconds) before requeuing failed tasks.
- If a task fails (e.g. OOM or timeout), the system naturally "cools down" before the next attempt, and a Telegram notification is sent alerting the operator of the delay.

### 4. Scheduler Queue Safety (`scheduler.py`)
- Refactored `scheduler.py` to route heavy scheduled tasks (like the Daily SM-2 Push) through the unified `LocalTaskQueue` instead of running them synchronously.
- This entirely eliminates the risk of `scheduler.py` crashing the system by triggering an LLM task concurrently with an `inbox_daemon` ingestion pipeline.

---

> [!TIP]
> **What to test next:** Try dropping a highly complex prompt or file into the inbox. You should see the `RouterAgent` log:
> `🗺️ [RouterAgent] 接力觸發: ... (Model: deepseek-r1:14b)`
> Also, if you run the exact same `temperature=0` prompt twice, the second run should instantly return with:
> `⚡ 命中語意快取 (Semantic Cache)，跳過推理。`

## 3. Tasks Executed

# Phase A: High-Impact Optimizations

> **Status:** Executing

- `[x]` **Task 1: Semantic Caching in `llm_client.py`**
  - `[x]` Initialize SQLite database connection in `OllamaClient`
  - `[x]` Implement cache read/write logic for deterministic calls (`temperature=0`)
  - `[x]` Support async generating methods

- `[x]` **Task 2: Context-Aware Routing in `router_agent.py`**
  - `[x]` Add LLM complexity assessment for incoming intents
  - `[x]` Map low-complexity to lightweight model (e.g. Qwen-7B)
  - `[x]` Pass `--model` flag in command arguments when enqueuing

- `[x]` **Task 3: Task Queue Exponential Backoff**
  - `[x]` Integrate `tenacity` retry backoff inside `task_queue.py` `_worker_loop`
  - `[x]` Handle robust subprocess failure backoff

- `[x]` **Task 4: Scheduler Queue Safety**
  - `[x]` Refactor `scheduler.py` to enqueue background tasks to `task_queue.py` instead of running directly
